BridgePoint Technical Note
HOWTO Update the BridgePoint Copyright


Abstract
--------
This note describes the steps to be performed in order to update the copyright
messages in BridgePoint to include a new year.

History
-------
None.

Document References
-------------------
[1] Bugzilla Issue 2673 
    http://phoenix.projtech.com/bugzilla/show_bug.cgi?id=2673
[2] cvs://Documentation/internal/process/templates/checklists/new-start.chk

Background
----------
With each new year it is necessary to update to copyright messages in the
BridgePoint source repository.  There is a utility for this purpose.  

Intended Audience
-----------------
This document is intended for the BridgePoint development team.

Steps
-----
x- You must have perl installed on your machine
x- Launch Eclipse
x- Update your development workspace with the latest version from HEAD of 
   all BridgePoint projects whose copyrights need to be updated.  This list
   can be obtained from the new-start checklist [2].
o- remove <cvs>Documentation from your workspace
    Note: You don't have to do this, but if you leave it it will update a lot of 
          things under Documentation that we really don't want to have updated 
          (archived notes).  If you choose to leave that folder, just replace 
          the files that you don't want to keep with the latest from your 
          branch.
          
          However, many documents under <cvs>Documentation/internal/process
          DO need to be updated. 
          
x- Checkout the cvs://utilities project in your workspace
xR The utility that is used to update copyright messages is
   cvs://utilities/update-copyright/update-copyright.pl
xR Note: This utility does have a usage screen.  To see it use the --help 
         option.
x- Open a shell
x- cd <development workspace>
x- ./<path>/update-copyright.pl --recursive --year YYYY ./
xR A message will be displayed when the procedure is complete and it will tell 
   you that a file named update-copyright-results.txt has been created.  This
   contains a report of the changes.
x- Examine the report and modify it (and the modified files) to remove:
    x- Items from the ./metadata folder
   x- Items that have 3rd party copyrights. Following are the ones I know of 
      currently.  These will need to be manaully "unchanged" after the
      update.
       x- pt_antlr/antrl/Tool.java
       x- utilities/update-copyright/update-copyright.pl (not all places with
          copyrights should be modified)
   x- Anything else you see in the report that you will not be checking-in
   
x- Commit the report to the CVS test_results folder.
x- Commit the modified files to the CVS repository by following normal check-in 
   procedures.
x- Run unit tests
x- Any files used by the build server, for example <cvs>Installer_MIP_MIMIC,
   must be manually copied to the build server.
